I've been coming here for years and it has to be some of the best tacos I've ever had. The night workers are really cool and they always hook you up.

Only thing that sucks is the rice, it's always hard so I can't reccomend it, and the tacos have recently gotten more expensive which sucks but I def think they're worth the price.

Overall great taco spot, it's open 24/7 so that's the cool part. Try to go on wednesdays since they have the tacos cheaper.<//Review>

<rate>1<//rate>< Text>
Used to be you were able to get good finds.  And if looked at the merchandise behind the counter there would be a few really wonderful items.
BUT not true anymore.  The regular merchandise on the floor is unremarkable, and sometimes the items are in poor condition.  The "good stuff" behind the counter is middle of the road at best.  And have retail prices on them.
I believe what has happened is that they pull most all of the good pieces that are donated and list them online.  At retail pricing.
Makes me wonder if they should still have "non-profit" status?  Non-profits are exempt from paying taxes retailers have to pay.
No fun going in the Goodwill anymore for me.
Lori Driscoll.<//Text>

I had been researching Class C‚Äôs  online, primarily looking for competitive pricing and a reputable service department- as a lot of dealers don‚Äôt want to service an RV purchased else where.  Therefore I wasn‚Äôt crazy about driving out of area to save a few bucks, and rather wanted piece of mind to service the RV locally when needed.  Simi Valley RV was our first stop on our way to Los Angeles.  We arrived at 930 AM on a Sunday, although they officially open at 10.  We parked on the lot and were able to browse the exterior of a few RVs, when Lance- an extremely nice salesman greeted us and cracked a joke about relieving him for a sales meeting.  He put us at ease right away, and I could tell we were going to get along from the beginning.  Lance spent the better part of 2-hours with us, answering questions while the kids were yelling and running all over the place.  Lance was very knowledgeable about his inventory and explained the benefits of each model.  We didn‚Äôt feel pressured nor hurried at any point.  We talked numbers and pricing near the end, but I wanted to ensure I was getting the best deal before going further.  While unable to negotiate much, Lance suggested I do my research if there was any doubt I wasn‚Äôt getting the best price and if I saw the same model elsewhere for lower; he would match it.  We left to look at a few other places, but my experience with Lance is what brought us back to Simi Valley RV; coupled with the fact their pricing is very competitive and I did not find the model listed for lower-anywhere within 1000 miles. That‚Äôs where Robin came in to assist, keeping me updated on her efforts as banks made financing offers throughout the following afternoon. I told Simi RV I wanted to pick the RV up within a day to take on our first trip. < review>
We dad a clogged branch waste line between the kitchen sink and main stack in a townhouse/condo. They came as agreed. The technician was friendly, neat, competent, and got the job done. He agreed, after some prodding, to a discounted price within the latitude given him by the company.

< Review>
Called Rescue Rooter late Sunday night about a major clog in my kitchen and appointment was set for early Monday. Robert came exactly at 8:30 and asked for my input to problem; ran the water to the 3 sink piping"s and told me exactly how he was going to attack it and the associated price.
